    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content--semana-spring-react---episódio-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#-semana-spring-react---episódio-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/devsuperior/bds-assets/main/ds/devsuperior-logo-small.png"><img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/devsuperior/bds-assets/main/ds/devsuperior-logo-small.png" alt="DevSuperior logo" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> Semana Spring React - Episódio 1</h1>

<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-passo-criar-projeto-spring-boot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#passo-criar-projeto-spring-boot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Passo: criar projeto Spring Boot</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Criar projeto Spring Boot no <code>Spring Initializr</code> com as seguintes dependências:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Web</li>
<li>JPA</li>
<li>H2</li>
<li>Postgres</li>
<li>Security</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Ajuste no arquivo pom.xml:</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-xml position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;plugin&gt;
	&lt;groupId&gt;org.apache.maven.plugins&lt;/groupId&gt;

	&lt;version&gt;3.1.0&lt;/version&gt;
&lt;/plugin&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">plugin</span>&gt;
	&lt;<span class="pl-ent">groupId</span>&gt;org.apache.maven.plugins&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">groupId</span>&gt;
	&lt;<span class="pl-ent">artifactId</span>&gt;maven-resources-plugin&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">artifactId</span>&gt;
	&lt;<span class="pl-ent">version</span>&gt;3.1.0&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">version</span>&gt;

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Botão direito no projeto -&gt; Maven -&gt; Update project (force update)</li>
</ul>

<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-passo-rotas" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#passo-rotas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Passo: Rotas</h3>

<li>Instalar React Router DOM</li>

<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="yarn add react-router-dom@6.2.1 @types/react-router-dom@5.3.2"><pre><code>yarn add react-router-dom@6.2.1 @types/react-router-dom@5.3.2
</code></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  BrowserRouter,
  Routes,
  Route
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import Listing from 'pages/Listing';
import Form from 'pages/Form';
import Navbar from &quot;components/Navbar&quot;;

function App() {
  return (
    &lt;BrowserRouter&gt;
      &lt;Navbar /&gt;
      &lt;Routes&gt;
        &lt;Route path=&quot;/&quot; element={&lt;Listing /&gt;} /&gt;
        &lt;Route path=&quot;/form&quot;&gt;
          &lt;Route path=&quot;:movieId&quot; element={&lt;Form /&gt;} /&gt;
        &lt;/Route&gt;
      &lt;/Routes&gt;
    &lt;/BrowserRouter&gt;
  );
}

<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-moviecard" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#moviecard"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>MovieCard</h4>
